svc_plus v.20120625
(System) Lists services/drivers in Services key by LastWrite times in a short format with warnings for type mismatches
^^^^ Indicates non-standard Type
<<<< Indicates Start mismatch for Driver
**** Indicates ObjectName mismatch for Driver
>>>> Indicates Start mismatch for Service
++++ Indicates nonstandard ObjectName for Service.

<<<< Indicates Start mismatch for Driver
**** Indicates ObjectName mismatch for Driver
>>>> Indicates Start mismatch for Service
++++ Indicates nonstandard ObjectName for Service.
